from(bucket: "k6")
|> range(start: v.timeRangeStart, stop: v.timeRangeStop)
|> filter(fn: (r) => r["_measurement"] == "group_duration")
|> filter(fn: (r) => r["_field"] == "value")
|> aggregateWindow(every: 10s, fn: mean, createEmpty: false)
|> keep(columns: ["group", "_value", "_time"])
